## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task involves modeling the population growth rate (dP/dt) as a function of time and current population size, which is a classic population dynamics problem. The relationship likely involves density-dependent growth models where the growth rate depends on the current population level.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- {'name': 'Exponential (Malthusian) growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P', 'scenario': 'Unlimited growth where rate is proportional to current population'}
- {'name': 'Logistic growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P)', 'scenario': 'Density-dependent growth with carrying capacity'}

- {'name': 'Theta-logistic growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2)', 'scenario': 'Generalized logistic with flexible curvature of density dependence'}

- {'name': 'Von Bertalanffy-type growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 - c2 * P', 'scenario': 'Balance between anabolic (power-law) and catabolic (linear) processes'}
- {'name': 'Richards growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) / c2', 'scenario': 'Generalized sigmoidal growth with asymmetry parameter'}
- {'name': 'Power-law growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P**c1', 'scenario': 'Nonlinear density-dependent growth with fractional exponent'}
- {'name': 'Beverton-Holt continuous analog', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) - c2 * P', 'scenario': 'Growth with density-dependent reproduction and constant mortality'}
- {'name': 'Time-dependent exponential growth', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * exp(c1 * t)', 'scenario': 'Growth rate changes exponentially with time (e.g., changing environment)'}
- {'name': 'Logistic with time-varying capacity', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P * exp(c2 * t))', 'scenario': 'Logistic growth with time-dependent carrying capacity'}
- {'name': 'Quadratic density dependence', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P**2', 'scenario': 'Simple polynomial density dependence in growth rate'}

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Density-dependent negative feedback → multiplicative factor (1 - P/K) or (1 - c*P) reducing growth at high population
- Allee effect (positive density dependence at low P) → cubic terms in P or multiplicative factor (P - c) introducing a lower threshold
- Logarithmic saturation in growth → log(K/P) or log(1 + c*P) terms reflecting diminishing returns
- Intrinsic growth proportionality → dP/dt must contain P as a multiplicative factor for per-capita rate models
- Fractional power of population → P**c with 0 < c < 1 for sub-linear scaling (surface-area limited growth)
- Time-dependent environmental forcing → multiplicative or additive functions of t (e.g., sin(c*t), exp(c*t)) modulating growth parameters
- Balance of gain and loss terms → difference of two positive terms (e.g., c0*P**a - c1*P**b) representing birth-death dynamics
- Carrying capacity signature → dP/dt = 0 at a nonzero P value, implying a root structure in the growth rate expression

- P^(1/3) (cube root)
- P*exp(-c*t) (exponential decay times P)

Let me check each candidate systematically.

**Candidate 1:** `P*c0 + P^c1*c2*t^c3 + c4 + c5*exp(c6*t)*log(P*c7+1)`
Has `t^c3` and `log(P*c7+1)` - these can't match P^(1/3) and P*exp(ct). No P² term either (unless from log expansion, but that's not exact).
Candidate 1 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 2:** `(P*c0 + c1 + (c2*t+c3)*(P²*c4 + P*c5 + c6*exp(c7*t) + c8))/(c2*t+c3)`
Expanding: P²*c4 + P*c5 + c6*exp(c7*t) + c8 + (P*c0+c1)/(c2*t+c3)
The term (P*c0+c1)/(c2*t+c3) can't produce P^(1/3) or P*exp(ct).
Candidate 2 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 3:** `P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*exp(c3*t) + c4*exp(c5*t) + c6`
Has P², P, P*exp(ct), exp(ct), constant. Missing P^(1/3). Can't match.
Candidate 3 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 4:** `(P*c0+c1+(c2*t+c3)*(P²*c4+P*c5+c6*exp(c7*t)))/(c2*t+c3)`
= P²*c4 + P*c5 + c6*exp(c7*t) + (P*c0+c1)/(c2*t+c3). Same issue as Candidate 2.
Candidate 4 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 5:** `P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*(c3+t)^(1/3) + c4*exp(c5*t) + c6`
Has P*(c3+t)^(1/3) instead of P^(1/3). Not equivalent.
Candidate 5 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 6:** `P*c0 + P*(P*c1 + c2*exp(c3*t)) + P^c4*c5`
= P²*c1 + P*(c0+c2*exp(c3*t)) + c5*P^c4
= P²*c1 + P*c0 + P*c2*exp(c3*t) + c5*P^c4
Setting c4=1/3: P² + P + P*exp(ct) + P^(1/3). This matches GT's basis functions!
Candidate 6 verdict: [MATCH]

**Candidate 7:** `P²*c0 + P*c1 + P^c2*c3*exp(c4*t) + c5*exp(c6*t)`
Has P^c2*exp(c4*t) which couples P power with exp(t). GT needs P*exp(ct) and P^(1/3) separately.
If c2=1: P²+P+P*exp(ct)+exp(ct). Missing P^(1/3).
Candidate 7 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 8:** `P²*c0 + P*c1 + c2*exp(c3*t) + c4 + c5*t*(P+c6)^c7`
Has t*(P+c6)^c7 - can't match P^(1/3) (no t dependence) or P*exp(ct).
Candidate 8 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 9:** Rational in P. Expanding: `(c0*t+c1)/(P*c2+c3) + P²*c4 + P*c5 + c6*exp(c7*t) + c8`. The first term is rational in P, can't produce P^(1/3).
Candidate 9 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 10:** `P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*t^c3 + c4*exp(c5*t) + c6`
Has P*t^c3 instead of P^(1/3). Not equivalent.
Candidate 10 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 11:** `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + P^c3*c4 + c5`
= P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + c4*P^c3 + c5
Missing P² term. Set c5=0, c3=1/3. We have P + P*exp(ct) + P^(1/3). No P² term.
Candidate 11 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 12:** Has sin term. Can't match P^(1/3).
Candidate 12 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 13:** Has log(P*c5+1). Not P^(1/3).
Candidate 13 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 14:** `(P*c0*(P*c4+c5) + P*(P*c1+c2*exp(c3*t))*(P*c4+c5) + c6)/(P*c4+c5)`
= P*c0 + P*(P*c1+c2*exp(c3*t)) + c6/(P*c4+c5)
= P²*c1 + P*c0 + P*c2*exp(c3*t) + c6/(P*c4+c5). Rational term in P, can't be P^(1/3).
Candidate 14 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 15:** Has exp(P^c5*c6). Not P^(1/3).
Candidate 15 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 16:** Expanding: `P*c0/(c1*t+c2) + P*(P*c3+P*c4*exp(c5*t)+c6) + c7/(c1*t+c2)`
= P²*c3 + P²*c4*exp(c5*t) + P*c6 + P*c0/(c1*t+c2) + c7/(c1*t+c2). Has P²*exp(t), not P*exp(t).
Candidate 16 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 17:** `P*(P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + c3) + P^c4*c5*exp(c6*t)`
= P²*c0 + P²*c1*exp(c2*t) + P*c3 + c5*P^c4*exp(c6*t)
Has P²*exp(t). GT doesn't have that. If c1=0: P²*c0 + P*c3 + c5*P^c4*exp(c6*t). Need P*exp(ct) and P^(1/3) separately.
If c4=1: P² + P + P*exp(ct). Missing P^(1/3). If c4=1/3: P² + P + P^(1/3)*exp(ct). Missing P*exp(ct).
Candidate 17 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 18:** `P²*c0 + P*c1 + c2*exp(c3*t) + c4*exp(c5*t)*log(P*c6+1)`
Has exp(t)*log(P+c) instead of P^(1/3). Not equivalent.
Candidate 18 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 19:** `(P²*c0 + (P+c1)*(P²*c2+P*c3+c4*exp(c5*t)+c6))/(P+c1)`
= P²*c0/(P+c1) + P²*c2 + P*c3 + c4*exp(c5*t) + c6 + ... Wait, let me expand properly.
Numerator: P²*c0 + P³*c2 + P²*c3 + P*c4*exp(c5*t) + P*c6 + P²*c1*c2 + P*c1*c3 + c1*c4*exp(c5*t) + c1*c6
Denominator: P+c1
This is a cubic/linear rational function. Can't simplify to match GT with P^(1/3).
Actually wait - if c0 = -c1*c2 (to cancel the P³ term)... Let me set c0 = 0 and see:
Numerator: (P+c1)*(P²*c2+P*c3+c4*exp(c5*t)+c6) = polynomial in P times (P+c1)
Result: P²*c2 + P*c3 + c4*exp(c5*t) + c6. No P^(1/3).
Candidate 19 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 20:** Similar rational structure. Expanding:
`(P*c0+c1)/(P*c2+c3) + P²*c4 + P*c5 + c6*exp(c7*t) + c8`
Rational in P, no P^(1/3).
Candidate 20 verdict: [NO MATCH]

Candidate 23 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 24:** `P*(P*c0+P*c1*exp(c2*t)+c3) + c4*exp(c5*t)*log(P*c6+1)`

Candidate 24 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 25:** `P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*exp(c3*t) + c4*exp(c5*t)`

**Candidate 26:** `P*c0 + P*(P*c1+c2*exp(c3*t)) + c4`
= P²*c1 + P*c0 + P*c2*exp(c3*t) + c4. Missing P^(1/3).
Candidate 26 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 27:** `P*(P*c0+c1*exp(c2*t)) + c3*P^c4*t^c5`
Has P^c4*t^c5 instead of P^(1/3). Can't set c5=0 because then it's just P^c4*c3 which could be P^(1/3). Wait - if c5=0, then c3*P^c4*1 = c3*P^c4. So we'd have P²*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + c3*P^(1/3). But missing P linear term! We have P*c1*exp(c2*t) but no standalone P term.
Actually GT = -0.01034*P² + 0.7124*P + 0.7124*P^(1/3) + 0.7124*P*exp(-0.03459*t)
Candidate 27 with c5=0: P²*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + c3*P^(1/3). Missing P term.
Candidate 27 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 28:** `P²*c0 + P*c1 + c2 + c3*log(P*c4+1) + c5*exp(c6*t)`
Has log(P+c) instead of P^(1/3). Not equivalent.
Candidate 28 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 29:** `P*(P*c0+P*c1*exp(c2*t)+c3) + P^c4*c5*t^c6`

If c1=0, c6=0: P²*c0 + P*c3 + c5*P^(1/3). Missing P*exp(ct).
If c6=0, keep c1: P²*(c0+c1*exp(c2*t)) + P*c3 + c5*P^(1/3). Has P²*exp(t), not P*exp(t).

**Candidate 31:** `P²*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*((P*c3)^c4-1) + c5*exp(c6*t) + c7`
= P²*c0 + P*c1 + c2*P*(c3^c4*P^c4-1) + c5*exp(c6*t) + c7
= P²*c0 + P*c1 + c2*c3^c4*P^(c4+1) - c2*P + c5*exp(c6*t) + c7
If c4 = -2/3: P^(1/3) term. Then c2*c3^(-2/3)*P^(1/3) - c2*P + P²*c0 + P*c1 + c5*exp(c6*t) + c7
= P²*c0 + P*(c1-c2) + c2*c3^(-2/3)*P^(1/3) + c5*exp(c6*t) + c7
This has P², P, P^(1/3), exp(ct), constant. But GT has P*exp(ct), not just exp(ct). Missing P*exp(ct).
